posted:Posted July 15, 2021
msg:Had a really good experience. Location is about 20-30 minutes from Pudong Airport and about the same amount of time to get to Disneyland park. Check-in was very quick. Showed passport, vaccination code, and green code and that was enough. 

Room was very comfortable. Electric curtains, also blackout, made for a great night sleep on the very comfy plush bed. Bath tub in the room was great for a soak (bath salts provided) after a long day of walking. 

Breakfast was okay. Mostly Chinese options with some western options (fried eggs, sausage, toast, cereal) available. Several restaurant's and room service also available, but didn't use them. There is also a spa on the b1 level but didn't have enough time to schedule something. 

Overall really good experience and would definitely stay there again.
